# 1. Accelerator ë¼ì´ë¸ŒëŸ¬ë¦¬

- Huggingface Pipelineì„ Langchainì—ì„œ ë¡œë“œí•  ë•Œ, ìƒê°ë³´ë‹¤ ì‰½ê²Œ êµ¬í˜„í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆê³  ë˜ ì¼ë¶€ëŠ” ì´ë¯¸ ì €í¬ ì½”ë“œì— í¬í•¨ì´ ë˜ì–´ ìˆëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ëª¨ë¸ ë¡œë“œ ì‹œ `device_map = "auto"`ë¡œ ì§€ì •í•˜ë©´ Accelerator ë¼ì´ë¸ŒëŸ¬ë¦¬ë¥¼ ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ê²Œ ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

```python
model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(MODEL_NAME, 
                                             torch_dtype=torch.bfloat16, 
                                             device_map="auto", # accelerator ì´ë¯¸ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ê³  ìˆìŒ.
                                             use_cache=True)
```

- vLLMì´ GPUë¥¼ ë³‘ë ¬ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ê±°ë‚˜ ë¹„ë™ê¸°ì²˜ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì‹œë„í•  ê²½ìš° ê³„ì†í•´ì„œ ë°˜ë³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì—ëŸ¬ë©”ì‹œì§€ë¥¼ ë±‰ëŠ”ë°, ì´ ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ í•´ê²°í•˜ì§€ ëª»í•˜ì˜€ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
- ë”°ë¼ì„œ, **vLLM ë¯¸ì‚¬ìš© + ë¹„ë™ê¸° ì²˜ë¦¬, ê·¸ë¦¬ê³  vLLM ì‚¬ìš© + ë™ê¸° ì²˜ë¦¬ì˜ ê²½ìš°ë¥¼ ë¹„êµ**í•  ê²ƒì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.

# 2. vLLM

- vLLMì€ ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ FlashAttentionì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤! ì‚¬ìš©í•´ë³´ì‹œë©´ FlashAttentionê³¼ XFormersê°€ ë°±ì—”ë“œì—ì„œ ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ í™•ì¸í•˜ì‹¤ ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤..
- ë°±ì—”ë“œ ë©”ì‹œì§€ì—ì„œ FlashAttentionì€ EXAONEê³¼ í˜¸í™˜ì´ ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ”ë‹¤ê³  ì¶œë ¥ë˜ë©°, XFormers ë¼ì´ë¸ŒëŸ¬ë¦¬ë¥¼ í˜¸ì¶œí•˜ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ í™•ì¸í•˜ì‹¤ ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
- cf. VLLM config

- êµ³ì´ FlashAttentionì„ ë”°ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©í•  í•„ìš”ê°€ ì—†ì–´ë³´ì—¬ì„œ, vLLMë§Œ ì‚¬ìš©í•œ ê²°ê³¼ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ìœ„ì—ì„œ ì„¤ëª…í•œ ë°”ì™€ ê°™ì´, vLLM ì‚¬ìš© + ë™ê¸°ì²˜ë¦¬ì˜ ê²½ìš°ì™€ vLLM ë¯¸ì‚¬ìš© + ë¹„ë™ê¸°ì²˜ë¦¬ì˜ ê²½ìš°ë¥¼ ë¹„êµí•´ë³´ì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
- ë˜í•œ ëª¨ë¸ì€ ì–´ì°¨í”¼ DaGë¥¼ ì‚¬ìš©í•  ê²ƒì´ë¼ê³  ìƒê°í•˜ì—¬ êµ³ì´ ëª¨ë¸ ê°„ ë¹„êµ ìˆ˜í–‰í•˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ê³ , `google/gemma-2-2b-it` 2Bì§œë¦¬ instruction tuned modelì„ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì—¬ Summarizationê³¼ final output ëª¨ë‘ ìƒì„±í•´ ëƒˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
- ì‘ì€ í¬ê¸°ì˜ ëª¨ë¸ì„ì—ë„ ê½¤ ì¤€ìˆ˜í•œ í€„ë¦¬í‹°ì˜ ë‹µë³€ì„ ë‚´ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ í™•ì¸í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤..!

- ì•„ë˜ì˜ ë‘ ê°€ì§€ ê²½ìš°ëŠ” ê¸°ë³¸ì ìœ¼ë¡œ `search_pipeline.py` ì™€ `final_output.py` íŒŒì¼ì—ì„œ í° ì°¨ì´ê°€ ìˆì§€ë§Œ, `summarizer.py` ì—ì„œë„ ë³€í™”ê°€ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

    async def summarize_task(doc):
            async with semaphore:

### 2.1. vLLM ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ëŠ” ê²½ìš°

- `jin/query_search_merged_exp/search` ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì—ì„œ `search_pipeline.py`  íŒŒì¼ê³¼ `final_output.py` íŒŒì¼ì„ ì°¸ê³ í•˜ì‹œë©´ ì•„ë˜ ë‚´ìš©ì„ í™•ì¸í•˜ì‹¤ ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
- ì‚¬ìš©í•œ ëª¨ë¸ : `"google/gemma-2-2b-it"`
- subquery : â€œë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼â€, â€œíŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”â€
- ëª¨ë¸ ë¡œë“œ
    
    ```python
    llm = VLLM(model = "google/gemma-2-2b-it",
                   trust_remote_code = True,
                   max_new_tokens = 128,
                   top_k = 10,
                   top_p = 0.95,
                   temperature = 0.9,
                   gpu_memory_utilization = 0.8, # OOM ë°©ì§€
                   max_num_seqs = 8 # batch size ì¡°ì •
                   # tensor_parallel_size = 4 # for distributed inference
            
        )
    ```
    
- ë””í…Œì¼í•œ ì½”ë“œ
    - ì˜¤ë¥˜ ì¡ê³  í•´ê²°í•˜ê¸° + ê°œì¸ ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì—ì„œ ë¹ ë¥´ê²Œ ì‘ì—…í•˜ëŠë¼ ê¹¨ë—í•œ ì½”ë“œëŠ” ì•„ë‹™ë‹ˆë‹¤ã… ã… 
    - ë°œí‘œ í›„ ì˜ˆì˜ê²Œ ë§Œë“¤ì–´ë†“ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
    - `search_pipeline.py`
        
        ```python
        # import search.serper as serper
        # import search.crawler as crawler
        import serper as serper
        import crawler as crawler
        import concurrent.futures
        # import search.summarizer as summarizer
        import summarizer as summarizer
        import asyncio
        from langchain_community.llms import VLLM
        from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
        from langchain_core.output_parsers import StrOutputParser
        import time
        import torch
        import torch.distributed as dist
        import atexit
        import os
        import re
        
        os.environ['MASTER_ADDR'] = 'localhost'  # ë˜ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë§ˆìŠ¤í„° ë…¸ë“œ IP ì£¼ì†Œ
        os.environ['MASTER_PORT'] = '12345'      # ì„ì˜ì˜ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ” í¬íŠ¸
        
        # queryì—ì„œ processed_queryë¥¼ ì•„ë˜ í˜•ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°›ì•„ì™”ìŒì„ ê°€ì •
        # processed_query = [
        #     {
        #         "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
        #         "routing": "web"
        #     },
        #     {
        #         "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
        #         "routing": "web"
        #     }
        # ]
        
        def filter_link(search_results):
            # ì–´ë–¤ ì œëª©ì˜ ë§í¬ë¥¼ íƒ€ê³  ë“¤ì–´ê°”ëŠ”ì§€ ê¸°ì–µí•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•´ dictionary ì‚¬ìš© (titleì„ key, linkë¥¼ valueë¡œ ì €ì¥)
            links_dict = {item['title']: item['link'] for search in search_results for item in search.get('organic', [])}
            return links_dict
        
        def crawl_links(filtered_links, crawler):
            crawled_data = {}
        
            for title, link in filtered_links.items():
                text = crawler.crawl(link)  # í¬ë¡¤ë§ ì‹¤í–‰
                crawled_data[title] = text  # íƒ€ì´í‹€ê³¼ í¬ë¡¤ë§ëœ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë”•ì…”ë„ˆë¦¬ë¡œ ì €ì¥
            final_results = {k: v for k, v in crawled_data.items() if v is not None}
            
            return final_results
        
        # ë³‘ë ¬ ì²˜ë¦¬ í•¨ìˆ˜
        def crawl_links_parallel(filtered_links, crawler):
            crawled_data = {}
            
            def fetch_data(title, link):
                text = crawler.crawl(link)
                return title, text
            
            with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as executor:
                future_to_title = {executor.submit(fetch_data, title, link): title for title, link in filtered_links.items()}
                
                for future in concurrent.futures.as_completed(future_to_title):
                    title, text = future.result()
                    if text is not None:
                        crawled_data[title] = text
            
            return crawled_data
        
        def search_pipeline(processed_query, llm):   
            if os.environ.get('WORLD_SIZE', '1') != '1':
                dist.init_process_group(backend='nccl', world_size=1, rank=0) 
            search_results = serper.serper_search(processed_query) # api í˜¸ì¶œ
            filtered_links = filter_link(search_results)
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            print("\n\n==============Search api Result==============\n")
            print(filtered_links)
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            final_results = crawl_links_parallel(filtered_links, crawler)
            print("\n\n==============Crawling Result==============\n")
            print(final_results)
            summarized_results = asyncio.run(summarizer.summarize(list(final_results.values()), llm))
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            print("\n\n==============Summarization Result==============\n")
            print(summarized_results)
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            
            return summarized_results
        
        # Test
        if __name__ == "__main__":
            processed_query = [
            {
                "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
                "routing": "web"
            },
            {
                "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
                "routing": "web"
            }
            ]
            
            llm = VLLM(model = "google/gemma-2-2b-it",
                       trust_remote_code = True,
                       max_new_tokens = 128,
                       top_k = 10,
                       top_p = 0.95,
                       temperature = 0.9,
                       gpu_memory_utilization = 0.8, # OOM ë°©ì§€
                       max_num_seqs = 8 # batch size ì¡°ì •
                       # tensor_parallel_size = 4 # for distributed inference
                
            )
        
            start_time = time.time()
            summarized_results = search_pipeline(processed_query, llm)
            end_time = time.time()
            
            print(summarized_results, f"Search ~ Summarization Execution Time: {end_time-start_time}")
        ```
        
    - `final_output.py`
        
        ```python
        import serper as serper
        import crawler as crawler
        import concurrent.futures
        import summarizer as summarizer
        import asyncio
        from langchain_community.llms import VLLM
        import time
        import torch
        import torch.distributed as dist
        import os, re
        from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
        from langchain_core.runnables import RunnableLambda
        from search_pipeline import search_pipeline
        from langchain_core.output_parsers import StrOutputParser
        
        # os.environ['MASTER_ADDR'] = 'localhost'  # ë˜ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë§ˆìŠ¤í„° ë…¸ë“œ IP ì£¼ì†Œ
        # os.environ['MASTER_PORT'] = '12345'      # ì„ì˜ì˜ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ” í¬íŠ¸
        
        # queryì—ì„œ processed_queryë¥¼ ì•„ë˜ í˜•ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°›ì•„ì™”ìŒì„ ê°€ì •
        # processed_query = [
        #     {
        #         "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
        #         "routing": "web"
        #     },
        #     {
        #         "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
        #         "routing": "web"
        #     }
        # ]
        
        if __name__ == "__main__":
            query = "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”ì— ëŒ€í•´ ì•Œë ¤ì¤˜"
        
            processed_query = [
            {
                "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
                "routing": "web"
            },
            {
                "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
                "routing": "web"
            }
            ]
            
            llm = VLLM(model = "google/gemma-2-2b-it",
                       trust_remote_code = True,
                       max_new_tokens = 512,
                       top_k = 10,
                       top_p = 0.95,
                       temperature = 0.9,
                       gpu_memory_utilization = 0.8, # OOM ë°©ì§€
                       max_num_seqs = 8 # batch size ì¡°ì •
                       # tensor_parallel_size = 4 # for distributed inference
                
            )
        
            summarized_results = search_pipeline(processed_query, llm)
            
            contexts = []
            for result in summarized_results:
                contexts.append(result['output_text'])
        
            prompt_template = PromptTemplate(
                input_variables=["context", "query"],
                template=f"""ì•„ë˜ ì •ë³´ì— ê¸°ë°˜í•˜ì—¬, ì‚¬ìš©ìì˜ ì§ˆë¬¸ì— ë‹µí•˜ì„¸ìš”.
                {contexts}
                ì‚¬ìš©ì ì§ˆë¬¸: {query} """
            )           
        
            chat_prompt = prompt_template.format(context="\n".join(contexts), query=query)
        
            # runnableë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ê¸°
            chat_runnable = RunnableLambda(lambda input: chat_prompt)
            
            chain = (
                chat_runnable
                | llm
                | StrOutputParser()
            )
        
            start_time = time.time()
            answer = chain.invoke(query)
            end_time = time.time()
        
            print(answer, f"Final Output Execution Time: {end_time-start_time}")
        ```
        

### **2.1.1. Search pipeline** (api ë¶ˆëŸ¬ì˜¤ê¸°, í¬ë¡¤ë§í•˜ê¸°, í¬ë¡¤ë§í•œ ë¬¸ì„œ ìš”ì•½í•˜ê¸°)

- **ì†Œìš” ì‹œê°„**
    - `Search ~ Summarization Execution Time: 10.23s`
- **ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼:**
    - ì§€í˜œ(ì‹¬)ë‹˜ê»˜ì„œ query routing ê´€ë ¨í•´ì„œëŠ” gemma2b model ì¶”ì²œí•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ”ë‹¤ê³  í•˜ì…¨ì§€ë§Œ, summarizationì€ ê·¸ë˜ë„ ê½¤ ì˜í•˜ëŠ” ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
    - ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì°¸ê³ 
        
        ```python
        ==============Summarization Result==============

ì„¤ê³„ì—, 3ë¶„ì˜ 1ì€ ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” ìŠ¤íŒŒê²Œí‹° ê´´ë¬¼ì£¼ì˜ì—, 3ë¶„ì˜ 1ì€ ì••ë„ì ì¸ ê´€ì°° ê°€ëŠ¥í•œ ì¦ê±°ì— ê¸°ì´ˆí•œ ë…¼ë¦¬ì  ì¶”ì¸¡ì— ì¨ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.\n\nêµìœ¡ìœ„ì›íšŒë¡œë¶€í„° ë‹µì¥ì´ ì—†ì ì¶œíŒì„ ìœ„í•´ í—¨ë”ìŠ¨ì—ê²Œ ì„ ê¸ˆ 8ë§Œ ë‹¬ëŸ¬ë¥¼ ì§€ë¶ˆí–ˆë‹¤.[5]\n\nì±…ì€ íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€íŒŒë¦¬ì•„ë‹ˆì¦˜ì˜ êµë¦¬ë¥¼ ì œì‹œí•˜ë©° ì°½ì¡° ì‹ í™”, ì „ë„ ì§€ì¹¨, FSMì˜ ì¡´ì¬ì— ëŒ€í•œ ìœ ì‚¬ê³¼í•™ì  ì¦ê±°, ì—¬ëŸ¬ íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ë§ì¥ë‚œì„ í¬í•¨í•œë‹¤.[3]ë³€ê²½ëœ ìŠ¤í†¡ ì‚¬ì§„ê³¼ ì¡°ì¡í•œ ê·¸ë¦¼ì„ ì´ìš©í•´ ì§„í™”ë¡ ì˜ ë¬¸ì œì ì„ ì§€ì í•˜ê³ , ì¸ë¥˜ ì—­ì‚¬ ì† íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€íŒŒë¦¬ì•„ë‹ˆì¦˜ì˜ ì¦ê±°ë¥¼ ì œì‹œí•˜ê³ , FSMì´ ìš°ë¦¬ê°€ ì‚¶ì„ ì–´ë–»ê²Œ ì‚´ê¸° ë°”ë¼ëŠ”ì§€ ê³µê°œí•œë‹¤.[6]ë˜í•œ í•´ì ì˜ ìˆ˜ê°€ ê°ì†Œí•¨ì— ë”°ë¼ ì§€êµ¬ì˜ ê¸°ì˜¨ì´ ìƒìŠ¹í–ˆë‹¤ê³  ì£¼ì¥í•œë‹¤. ë§ì€ ì‚¬ëŒë“¤ì´ í• ë¡œìœˆì— í•´ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ë³€ì¥í•˜ê³ , 10ì›” 31ì¼ ë‹¤ìŒì€ ì´ì „ë³´ë‹¤ ì¼ë°˜ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì¶”ìš´ ê²ƒì„ ì´ ì£¼ì¥ì˜ ê·¼ê±°ë¡œ ì œì‹œí•œë‹¤. ì´ëŠ” ìƒê´€ê´€ê³„ê°€ ì¸ê³¼ê´€ê³„ë¥¼ ì˜ë¯¸í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ”ë‹¤ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ ë³´ì—¬ì£¼ê¸° ìœ„í•œ ê²ƒì´ë‹¤.[7]\n\nì±…ì€ "ë‹¹ì‹ ì´ ìš°ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì¢‹ì•„í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ”ë‹¤ë©´, ë‹¹ì‹ ì˜ ì›ë˜ ì¢…êµê°€ ë‹¹ì‹ ì„ ë‹¤ì‹œ ë°ë ¤ê°ˆ ê²ƒ"ì´ë¼ê³  ë§í•˜ë©° ë…ìë“¤ì—ê²Œ 30ì¼ ë™ì•ˆ íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€íŒŒë¦¬ì•„ë‹ˆì¦˜ì„ ì‹œë„í•  ê²ƒì„ ê¶Œìœ í•œë‹¤.[8]\n\në³´ì´ì§€ ì•Šê³  ê°ì§€í•  ìˆ˜ ì—†ëŠ” FSMì€ ìš°ì£¼ë¥¼ ì°½ì¡°í–ˆë‹¤.[9]ì²«ì§¸ ë‚ ì—ëŠ” ì–´ë‘ ì—ì„œ ë¹›ì„ ë¶„ë¦¬í–ˆë‹¤. ë¹„í–‰ì— ì§€ì¹˜ê³  ë¬¼ì„ ì˜¤ë«ë™ì•ˆ ë°Ÿì§€ ëª»í•´ ë‘˜ì§¸ ë‚ ì—ëŠ” ë§¥ì£¼ í™”ì‚°ì´ ìˆëŠ” ë•…ì„ ì°½ì¡°í–ˆë‹¤. ë§¥ì£¼ë¥¼ ë§›ë³¸ í›„ ì…‹ì§¸ ë‚ ì—ëŠ” ìˆ™ì·¨ê°€ ìˆëŠ” ì±„ë¡œ ê¹¨ì–´ë‚¬ë‹¤. ì „ë‚ ì— ë•…ì„ ë§Œë“¤ì—ˆë‹¤ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ ìŠì–´ë²„ë ¤ì„œ ë‹¤ì‹œ ë•…ì„ ì°½ì¡°í•œ í›„ ë‘˜ì§¸ ë‚ ì˜ ë•…ì„ ì²œêµ­ìœ¼ë¡œ ì˜¬ë ¸ë‹¤. ì´í›„ ë‚œìŸì´ë¥¼ ì°½ì¡°í•´ ì´ë¥¼ ì¸ê°„ì´ë¼ê³  ë¶ˆë €ë‹¤.[10]\n\nì±…ì€ ì°½ì¡°ëŠ” 5ì²œ ë…„ ì „ì— ì¼ì–´ë‚¬ìœ¼ë‚˜, FSMì´ ìš°ë¦¬ë¥¼ ì†ì´ê¸° ìœ„í•´ ê³¼í•™ì  ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ë°”ê¿¨ë‹¤ê³  ì£¼ì¥í•œë‹¤. ë˜í•œ íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€íŒŒë¦¬ì•„ë‹ˆì¦˜ì€ ì§€ì  ì„¤ê³„ì²˜ëŸ¼ ê²°ë¡ ì„ ë¨¼ì € ë‚´ë¦¬ê³  ì´ë¥¼ ë’·ë°›ì¹¨í•  ì¦ê±°ë¥¼ ëª¨ì€ë‹¤ê³  ì„¤ëª…í•œë‹¤.[11]\n\nëª¨ì§€ ì„ ì¥ì€ FSMìœ¼ë¡œë¶€í„° ì¡°ì–¸ì„ ë‹´ì€ 10ê°œì˜ ì„íŒì„ ë°›ì•˜ìœ¼ë‚˜, 2ê°œëŠ” ì‚´ì‚¬ì‚°ì—ì„œ ë‚´ë ¤ì˜¤ëŠ” ê¸¸ì— ë–¨ì–´ì¡Œë‹¤. ì´ ì‚¬ê±´ì€ "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€íŒŒë¦¬ì•ˆë“¤ì˜ ì–´ì„¤í”ˆ ë„ë• ê¸°ì¤€ì„ ë¶€ë¶„ì ìœ¼ë¡œ í‰í–ˆë‹¤.[6]ã€Šë°ì¼ë¦¬ í…”ë ˆê·¸ë˜í”„ã€‹ì˜ì‚¬ì´ë¨¼ ì‹±ì€ ì±…ì´ ì•½ê°„ ë°˜ë³µì ì´ë‚˜, ì „ë°˜ì ìœ¼ë¡œ "í›Œë¥­í•˜ê³  ë„ë°œì ì´ë©° ì¬ì¹˜ ìˆê³  ì¤‘ìš”í•œ ë³´ì„"ì´ë¼ê³  ì¹­ì°¬í–ˆë‹¤.[9]í•œí¸ë””ìŠ¤ì»¤ë²„ë¦¬ ì—°êµ¬ì†Œì˜ ì¼€ì´ì‹œ ëŸ¬ìŠ¤í‚¨ì€ ì±…ì´ì‹ ì•½ì„±ê²½ì„ ì¡°ë¡±í•œë‹¤ê³  ë¹„íŒí–ˆë‹¤.[13]')], 'output_text': '\n\nThe "Gospel of the Flying Spaghetti Monster" is a satirical book that uses humor to poke fun at intelligent design. Bobby Henderson, who wrote the book, presents the FSM\'s beliefs as a parody and argues that the FSM is a real being. Though initially a joke, the book became popular and is now a widely discussed topic.  Critics say it lacks serious theological depth, while others find its approach engaging and insightful.  \n'}]
        ```
        

### **2.1.2. ìš”ì•½ëœ ì •ë³´ë¥¼ ê°€ì§€ê³  ìµœì¢… ë‹µë³€ ìƒì„±í•˜ê¸°**

- ì†Œìš” ì‹œê°„
    - `Final Output Execution Time: 1.02s`
- **ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼** (êµ¬ì¡°í™”ëœ ë°ì´í„°ì²˜ëŸ¼ ë³´ì´ì§€ëŠ” ì•Šì§€ë§Œ, ë‹¨ìˆœí•œ ì¿¼ë¦¬ì—¬ì„œ ê·¸ëŸ° ê²ƒ ê°™ê¸°ë„ í•˜ê³ .. ì‘ì€ ëª¨ë¸ ì¹˜ê³ ëŠ” ê½¤ ê´œì°®ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.)
    
    ë‹µë³€: ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”ëŠ” 2005ë…„ì— ìƒì„±ëœ ë†ë‹´ê³¼ ê´€ë ¨ëœ ì¢…êµì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. ì¸ê°„ì€ ì¸ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ìƒë¬¼í•™ì  ìœ ì „ìë¥¼ ì¡°ì‘í•˜ëŠ” ê²ƒì„ ì˜¹í˜¸í•˜ëŠ” ì‹ ë…ì´ë¼ëŠ” ì£¼ì œì—ì„œ íƒ„ìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.  ê·¸ê²ƒì€ ì¸ìƒì˜ ì¦ê±°ì›€ê³¼ ì‚¶ì˜ ì¦ê±°ì›€ì„ ì˜¹í˜¸í•˜ëŠ” ë° ì¤‘ì ì„ ë‘¡ë‹ˆë‹¤. ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”ëŠ” ì§€ì†ì ì¸ ì‹ ë…, ì „í˜•ì ì¸ ì‹ ì•™ê³¼ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ê²ƒìœ¼ë¡œ ë¬˜ì‚¬ë©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
    

### 2.2. vLLM ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ” ê²½ìš°

`jin/query_search_merged_exp/search_without_vllm` ë””ë ‰í† ë¦¬ì—ì„œ ê°™ì€ ì´ë¦„ì˜ íŒŒì¼ `final_output.py`ì™€ `search_pipeline.py`ë¡œ ì‘ì—… ë‚´ìš©ì„ í™•ì¸í•˜ì‹¤ ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. 

- ë””í…Œì¼í•œ ì½”ë“œ
    - `search_pipeline.py`
        
        ```python
        # import search.serper as serper
        # import search.crawler as crawler
        import serper as serper
        import crawler as crawler
        import concurrent.futures
        # import search.summarizer as summarizer
        import summarizer as summarizer
        import asyncio
        from langchain_community.llms import VLLM
        from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
        from langchain_core.output_parsers import StrOutputParser
        import time
        import torch
        import torch.distributed as dist
        import atexit
        import os
        import re
        from transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, pipeline
        from langchain.llms import HuggingFacePipeline
        
        os.environ['MASTER_ADDR'] = 'localhost'  # ë˜ëŠ” ì‹¤ì œ ë§ˆìŠ¤í„° ë…¸ë“œ IP ì£¼ì†Œ
        os.environ['MASTER_PORT'] = '12345'      # ì„ì˜ì˜ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì§€ ì•ŠëŠ” í¬íŠ¸
        
        # queryì—ì„œ processed_queryë¥¼ ì•„ë˜ í˜•ì‹ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°›ì•„ì™”ìŒì„ ê°€ì •
        # processed_query = [
        #     {
        #         "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
        #         "routing": "web"
        #     },
        #     {
        #         "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
        #         "routing": "web"
        #     }
        # ]
        
        def filter_link(search_results):
            # ì–´ë–¤ ì œëª©ì˜ ë§í¬ë¥¼ íƒ€ê³  ë“¤ì–´ê°”ëŠ”ì§€ ê¸°ì–µí•˜ê¸° ìœ„í•´ dictionary ì‚¬ìš© (titleì„ key, linkë¥¼ valueë¡œ ì €ì¥)
            links_dict = {item['title']: item['link'] for search in search_results for item in search.get('organic', [])}
            return links_dict
        
        def crawl_links(filtered_links, crawler):
            crawled_data = {}
        
            for title, link in filtered_links.items():
                text = crawler.crawl(link)  # í¬ë¡¤ë§ ì‹¤í–‰
                crawled_data[title] = text  # íƒ€ì´í‹€ê³¼ í¬ë¡¤ë§ëœ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë”•ì…”ë„ˆë¦¬ë¡œ ì €ì¥
            final_results = {k: v for k, v in crawled_data.items() if v is not None}
            
            return final_results
        
        # ë³‘ë ¬ ì²˜ë¦¬ í•¨ìˆ˜
        def crawl_links_parallel(filtered_links, crawler):
            crawled_data = {}
            
            def fetch_data(title, link):
                text = crawler.crawl(link)
                return title, text
            
            with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as executor:
                future_to_title = {executor.submit(fetch_data, title, link): title for title, link in filtered_links.items()}
                
                for future in concurrent.futures.as_completed(future_to_title):
                    title, text = future.result()
                    if text is not None:
                        crawled_data[title] = text
            
            return crawled_data
        
        def search_pipeline(processed_query, llm):   
            if os.environ.get('WORLD_SIZE', '1') != '1':
                dist.init_process_group(backend='nccl', world_size=1, rank=0) 
            search_results = serper.serper_search(processed_query) # api í˜¸ì¶œ
            filtered_links = filter_link(search_results)
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            print("\n\n==============Search api Result==============\n")
            print(filtered_links)
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            final_results = crawl_links_parallel(filtered_links, crawler)
            print("\n\n==============Crawling Result==============\n")
            print(final_results)
            summarized_results = asyncio.run(summarizer.summarize(list(final_results.values()), llm))
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            print("\n\n==============Summarization Result==============\n")
            print(summarized_results)
            if dist.is_initialized():
                dist.destroy_process_group()
            
            return summarized_results
        
        # Test
        if __name__ == "__main__":
            processed_query = [
            {
                "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
                "routing": "web"
            },
            {
                "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
                "routing": "web"
            }
            ]
            
            model_name = "google/gemma-2-2b-it"
            model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_name,
                                                    torch_dtype=torch.bfloat16, 
                                                     device_map="auto", # accelerator ì´ë¯¸ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ê³  ìˆìŒ.
                                                     use_cache=True)
            tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)
            
            text_gen_pipeline = pipeline(
                "text-generation",
                model=model,
                tokenizer=tokenizer,
                max_new_tokens=512,  # ì›í•˜ëŠ” ìµœëŒ€ í† í° ê¸¸ì´ ì„¤ì •
                temperature=0.7,
                top_k=50,
                top_p=0.95,
                repetition_penalty=1.2
            )
            
            # Langchainì— ë„£ì–´ì£¼ê¸° ìœ„í•´ì„œ pipelineìœ¼ë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ê¸°
            llm = HuggingFacePipeline(pipeline=text_gen_pipeline)
            
        
            start_time = time.time()
            summarized_results = search_pipeline(processed_query, llm)
            end_time = time.time()
            
            print(summarized_results, f"Search ~ Summarization Execution Time: {end_time-start_time}")
        ```
        
    - `final_output.py`
        
        ```
        import serper as serper
        import crawler as crawler
        import concurrent.futures
        import summarizer as summarizer
        import asyncio
        import time
        import torch
        import torch.distributed as dist
        import os, re
        from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
        from langchain_core.runnables import RunnableLambda
        from search_pipeline import search_pipeline
        from langchain_core.output_parsers import StrOutputParser
        from transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, pipeline
        from langchain.llms import HuggingFacePipeline
        
        if __name__ == "__main__":
            query = "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”ì— ëŒ€í•´ ì•Œë ¤ì¤˜"
        
            processed_query = [
            {
                "subquery": "ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼",
                "routing": "web"
            },
            {
                "subquery": "íŒŒìŠ¤íƒ€ ê´´ë¬¼ ì‹ í™”",
                "routing": "web"
            }
            ]
            model_name = "google/gemma-2-2b-it"
            model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_name,
                                                    torch_dtype=torch.bfloat16, 
                                                     device_map="auto", # accelerator ì‚¬ìš©ìš©.
                                                     use_cache=True)
            tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)
            
            text_gen_pipeline = pipeline(
                "text-generation",
                model=model,
                tokenizer=tokenizer,
                max_length=512,  
                max_new_tokens=256,  # 512 > 256
                temperature=0.7,
                top_k=50,
                top_p=0.95,
                repetition_penalty=1.2
            )
            
            # Langchainì— ë„£ì–´ì£¼ê¸° ìœ„í•´ì„œ pipelineìœ¼ë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ê¸°
            llm = HuggingFacePipeline(pipeline=text_gen_pipeline)
            
            
            # Summarization ê±°ì¹œ ê²°ê³¼ë¬¼
            summarized_results = search_pipeline(processed_query, llm)
            
            contexts = []
            for result in summarized_results:
                contexts.append(result['output_text'])
        
            prompt_template = PromptTemplate(
                input_variables=["context", "query"],
                template=f"""ì•„ë˜ ì •ë³´ì— ê¸°ë°˜í•˜ì—¬, ì‚¬ìš©ìì˜ ì§ˆë¬¸ì— ë‹µí•˜ì„¸ìš”.
                {contexts}
                ì‚¬ìš©ì ì§ˆë¬¸: {query} """
            )           
        
            chat_prompt = prompt_template.format(context="\n".join(contexts), query=query)
        
            # runnableë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ê¸°
            chat_runnable = RunnableLambda(lambda input: chat_prompt)
            
            chain = (
                chat_runnable
                | llm
                | StrOutputParser()
            )
        
            start_time = time.time()
            answer = chain.invoke(query)
            end_time = time.time()
        
            print(answer, f"Execution Time: {end_time-start_time}")
        ```
        

### **2.2.1. Search pipeline** (api ë¶ˆëŸ¬ì˜¤ê¸°, í¬ë¡¤ë§í•˜ê¸°, í¬ë¡¤ë§í•œ ë¬¸ì„œ ìš”ì•½í•˜ê¸°)

- ì†Œìš” ì‹œê°„ : ì—„ì²­ ê¸¸ì–´ì§‘ë‹ˆë‹¤..
    - `Search ~ Summarization Execution Time: 82.19s`
- ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼
    - ì™œì¸ì§€ ëª¨ë¥´ê² ëŠ”ë°.. ê°™ì€ ë¬¸ì„œê°€ ë‘ ë²ˆ ë‚˜ì˜¤ë„¤ìš”..? ì œê°€ ë­”ê°€ ì‹¤ìˆ˜ í–ˆì„ì§€ë„..
        - ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì°¸ê³ 
            
            ```python

He argues this is necessary for students to understand "the full spectrum of human thought," and he has sent letters to Kansas Education Committee members urging them to do so. His argument gained attention online, with his website receiving widespread traffic and even praise from some religious scholars who saw it as evidence supporting their own views on creationism. However, critics argue that teaching creationism alongside evolution would be scientifically inaccurate and misleading. The article highlights the controversy surrounding Henderson\'s request and its implications for science education.\n"\n\n\nCONCISE SUMMARY:\n\nA physics professor at Oregon State University wants public school teachers to teach both creationism and evolution in biology class. The process involves eating noodles (ramen), saying "ramen!" in gratitude, and mimicking the act of receiving spiritual guidance through this ritualistic meal. He argues this is necessary for students to understand "the full spectrum of human thought," and he has sent letters to Kansas Education Committee members urging them to do so. His argument gained attention online, with his website receiving widespread traffic and even praise from some religious scholars who saw it as evidence supporting their own views on creationism. However, critics argue that teaching creationism alongside evolution would be scientifically inaccurate and misleading. responsible for Earth\'s climate change and encourages its followers to embrace environmentalism through their actions. individuals and institutions to include creationist ideas in public school science curriculum.     - max length ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìƒê²¨ `summarizer.py` ì— ë¬¸ì„œë¥¼ ë¶„í• í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆëŠ” ì½”ë“œë¥¼ ì¶”ê°€í•˜ì˜€ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
        - ë¬¸ì„œ ë¶„í•  ì½”ë“œ
            
            ```python
            # ë¬¸ì„œ ë¶„í• ê¸° (ì¶”ê°€í•œ ë¶€ë¶„)
            def split_docs_by_token_count(docs, max_tokens):
                # LLMì˜ ìµœëŒ€ í† í° ìˆ˜ì— ë§ì¶° ë¬¸ì„œ ë¶„í• 
                splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(chunk_size=max_tokens, chunk_overlap=50)
                split_docs = []
                for doc in docs:
                    split_docs.extend(splitter.split_text(doc))
                return split_docs
            ```
            
        - ìˆ˜ì •ëœ `summarizer.py` ì „ì²´ ì½”ë“œ
            
            ```python
            from langchain.chains.summarize import load_summarize_chain
            from langchain.prompts import PromptTemplate
            from langchain.schema import Document
            from langchain_community.llms import HuggingFacePipeline
            from transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, pipeline
            import torch
            import time
            import asyncio
            import torch.distributed as dist
            import atexit
            from langchain.text_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter # ì¶”ê°€
            
            # ë¬¸ì„œ ë¶„í• ê¸° (ì¶”ê°€í•œ ë¶€ë¶„)
            def split_docs_by_token_count(docs, max_tokens):
                # LLMì˜ ìµœëŒ€ í† í° ìˆ˜ì— ë§ì¶° ë¬¸ì„œ ë¶„í• 
                splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(chunk_size=max_tokens, chunk_overlap=50)
                split_docs = []
                for doc in docs:
                    split_docs.extend(splitter.split_text(doc))
                return split_docs
            
            async def summarize(docs, llm, max_tokens=1000, max_concurrent_tasks=5):
                if not dist.is_initialized():
                    dist.init_process_group(backend="nccl", world_size=1, rank=0)
                    
                """HuggingFace LLMìœ¼ë¡œ ë¹„ë™ê¸°ì  ìš”ì•½ì„ ì‹¤í–‰"""
                if not docs:
                    return {}
            
                prompt_template = PromptTemplate(
                    input_variables=["text"],
                    template="""ë‹¤ìŒ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì½ê³ , ì£¼ìš” ì•„ì´ë””ì–´ì™€ í•µì‹¬ ë‚´ìš©ì„ íŒŒì•…í•˜ì—¬, ê°„ê²°í•˜ë©´ì„œë„ ëª…í™•í•œ ìš”ì•½ë¬¸ì„ ì‘ì„±í•´ ì£¼ì„¸ìš”.
            
                    ìš”ì•½ë¬¸ì€ ë‹¤ìŒ í•­ëª©ë“¤ì„ í¬í•¨í•´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤:
                    1. ë¬¸ì„œì˜ ì£¼ìš” ì£¼ì œ ë° ëª©ì 
                    2. í•µì‹¬ ë‚´ìš©ê³¼ ì¤‘ìš”í•œ ì„¸ë¶€ì‚¬í•­
                    3. ê²°ë¡  ë° ì „ë‹¬í•˜ê³ ì í•˜ëŠ” ë©”ì‹œì§€
            
                    ì™¸ë¶€ ì •ë³´ë¥¼ í¬í•¨í•˜ì§€ ì•Šê³  ì œê³µëœ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ì—ë§Œ ì „ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì˜ì¡´í•˜ì„¸ìš”.
                    
                    {text}"""
                )
            
                # ìš”ì•½ ì²´ì¸ ë¡œë”©
                chain = load_summarize_chain(llm, chain_type="map_reduce", return_intermediate_steps=False)
            
                # ë¹„ë™ê¸° ì‘ì—…ì˜ ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ì œí•œí•˜ëŠ” ì„¸ë§ˆí¬ì–´ë¥¼ ì„¤ì •í•˜ì—¬ ë™ì‹œì— ì‹¤í–‰ë˜ëŠ” ì‘ì—…ì˜ ìˆ˜ë¥¼ max_concurrent_tasksë¡œ ì œí•œí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
                semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrent_tasks)
            
                # ë¬¸ì„œ ë¶„í• 
                split_docs = split_docs_by_token_count(docs, max_tokens) # ì¶”ê°€í•œ ë¶€ë¶„
                
                # ê° ë¬¸ì„œë¥¼ ë°›ì•„ì˜¨ í›„ ìš”ì•½ ì‘ì—…ì„ ìˆ˜í–‰í•˜ëŠ” ë¹„ë™ê¸° í•¨ìˆ˜ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤
                # vllmê³¼ì˜ ì¶©ëŒ ë¬¸ì œ ë•Œë¬¸ì—, ìš°ì„  ainvoke ì œì™¸í•˜ì—¬ ì‹¤í–‰í•˜ì˜€ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
                async def summarize_task(doc):
                    async with semaphore:
                        #return await chain.ainvoke({"input_documents": [Document(page_content=doc)]})
                        return chain.invoke({"input_documents": [Document(page_content=doc)]})
                # ë¹„ë™ê¸°ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ìš”ì•½ ì‘ì—…ì„ ì‹¤í–‰í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤
                summaries = await asyncio.gather(*[summarize_task(doc) for doc in split_docs]) # ìˆ˜ì •í•œ ë¶€ë¶„ (docs > split_docs)
                def cleanup():
                    if dist.is_initialized():
                        dist.destroy_process_group()
                
                atexit.register(cleanup)
                
                return summaries  # ìš”ì•½ëœ ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ í˜•íƒœë¡œ ë°˜í™˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
            
            ```
            

### **2.2.2. ìš”ì•½ëœ ì •ë³´ë¥¼ ê°€ì§€ê³  ìµœì¢… ë‹µë³€ ìƒì„±í•˜ê¸°**

- ëª¨ë¸ ë¡œë“œ ì‹œ max length ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë°œìƒí•˜ì—¬ ì•„ë˜ì™€ ê°™ì´ í•˜ì´í¼íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ë¥¼ ì¡°ì •í•˜ì˜€ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤
    - max_new_tokens, max_length ì¡°ì •
        
        ```python
        model_name = "google/gemma-2-2b-it"
            model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_name,
                                                    torch_dtype=torch.bfloat16, 
                                                     device_map="auto", # accelerator ì‚¬ìš©ìš©.
                                                     use_cache=True)
            tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)
            
            text_gen_pipeline = pipeline(
                "text-generation",
                model=model,
                tokenizer=tokenizer,
                max_length=512,  
                max_new_tokens=256,  # 512 > 256
                temperature=0.7,
                top_k=50,
                top_p=0.95,
                repetition_penalty=1.2
            )
            
            # Langchainì— ë„£ì–´ì£¼ê¸° ìœ„í•´ì„œ pipelineìœ¼ë¡œ ê°ì‹¸ê¸°
            llm = HuggingFacePipeline(pipeline=text_gen_pipeline)
        ```
        
- ì†Œìš” ì‹œê°„ : ë˜ ì—„ì²­ ê¸¸ì–´ì§‘ë‹ˆë‹¤. `Execution Time: 14.89s`
- ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼
    - í”„ë¡¬í”„íŠ¸ë¥¼ ë‹µë³€ ë‚´ìš©ì— í¬í•¨í•˜ëŠ” ë“±, ì œëŒ€ë¡œ ì²˜ë¦¬í•˜ì§€ ëª»í•˜ëŠ” ëª¨ìŠµì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. ì œê°€ ë­”ê°€ ëª¨ë¸ íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸ì„ ë°”ê¾¸ë©´ì„œ ë¬¸ì œê°€ ìƒê²¼ì„ ìˆ˜ë„ ìˆì„ ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
    - max length ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë‹µë³€ ìƒì„±ì—ì„œë„ ë°œìƒí•˜ì˜€ëŠ”ë°ìš”, **vLLM ì—†ì´ ì‹¤í–‰í•˜ì˜€ì„ ë•Œ í™•ì‹¤íˆ ë©”ëª¨ë¦¬ë¥¼ íš¨ìœ¨ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì‚¬ìš©í•˜ì§€ ëª»í•œë‹¤**ëŠ” ì¸ì‚¬ì´íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì–»ì„ ìˆ˜ ìˆì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.
        - ì‹¤í–‰ ê²°ê³¼ ì°¸ê³ 
            
            ```python
            ì•„ë˜ ì •ë³´ì— ê¸°ë°˜í•˜ì—¬, ì‚¬ìš©ìì˜ ì§ˆë¬¸ì— ë‹µí•˜ì„¸ìš”.
            ['Write a concise summary of the following:\n\n\n"Write a concise summary of the following:\n\n\n"ì´ ì¢…êµê°€ ì™œ ì´ë ‡ê²Œ ìš°ìŠ¤ê½ìŠ¤ëŸ¬ìš´ ëª¨ìŠµì„ í•˜ê³  ìˆëŠ”ì§€ëŠ” ê·¸ íƒ„ìƒ ë°°ê²½ê³¼ ì„¤ë¦½ ëª©ì ì—ì„œ ì‚´í´ë³¼ ìˆ˜ ìˆë‹¤. ë¯¸êµ­ì˜\nìº”ììŠ¤\nì£¼ì—ì„œ\nì°½ì¡°ì„¤\nì‹ ë´‰ìë“¤ì´\nì§€ì ì„¤ê³„\në¥¼ í•„ìˆ˜ê³¼ëª©ì— í¬í•¨í•˜ìë©° ê°•í•˜ê²Œ ì£¼ì¥ì„ í•œ ì ì´ ìˆì—ˆëŠ”ë°, ê·¸ì¤‘ì— ìº”ììŠ¤ êµìœ¡ ìœ„ì›íšŒê°€ ê³µë¦½í•™êµì˜ ìƒë¬¼í•™ ìˆ˜ì—…ì—ì„œ ì§€ì  ì„¤ê³„ì™€ ì§„í™”ë¥¼ ë™ë“±í•˜ê²Œ ê°€ë¥´ì³ì•¼ í•œë‹¤ëŠ” ì£¼ì¥ì„ í•˜ì, 2005ë…„ ë‹¹ì‹œ\nì˜¤ë¦¬ê±´ ì£¼ë¦½ëŒ€í•™êµ\n[22]\nì—ì„œ\në¬¼ë¦¬í•™\nì„ ì „ê³µí•œ 25ì„¸ ì²­ë…„ ë°”ë¹„ í—¨ë”ìŠ¨(Bobby Henderson, 1980~)ì´ ì •ì²´ê°€ ëª¨í˜¸í•œ ì§€ì ì„¤ê³„ì ëŒ€ì‹  ì–´ë–¤ ì¡´ì¬ë¥¼ ì œì‹œí•´ë„ ë§ˆì°¬ê°€ì§€ë¼ê³  ì£¼ì¥í•˜ì˜€ë‹¤. ê·¸ëŸ¬ë©´ì„œ ì œì‹œí•œ ê²ƒì´ Flying Spaghetti Monster(FSM, ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” ìŠ¤íŒŒê²Œí‹° ê´´ë¬¼)ì´ì—ˆë‹¤. FSM êµë„ë“¤ì€ ì§„ì§€í•˜ê²Œ FSMì„ ë¯¿ëŠ”ë‹¤ê³  ì£¼ì¥í•˜ë©° ìŠ¤ìŠ¤ë¡œ FSM êµë„ë¡œ ìì²˜í•˜ê³  ìˆìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ ê·¸ ì†ì…ˆì´ ì–´ì°Œ ë˜ì—ˆë“  ê°„ì— ë”±íˆ FSMì„ ì¢…êµê°€ ì•„ë‹ˆë¼ê³  ê·œì •í•  ìˆ˜ ì—†ëŠ” ì…ˆì´ë‹¤.\nâ–² ìƒìˆ ëœ ì„œì‹ ì—ì„œ í•¨ê»˜ ì²¨ë¶€ëœ ê·¸ë¦¼. midg\ne\ntì´ ì•„ë‹ˆë¼ midg\ni\ntì´ë¼ê³  ì í˜€ ìˆë‹¤."\n\n\nCONCISE SUMMARY:\n\nThe text discusses the rise and recognition of "Flying Spaghetti Monster (FSM)" as an official religion in several countries. intelligent design, alongside evolution in biology classes. He argues this is necessary for equal treatment and believes it should be taught as an alternative explanation to evolution. His request was met with mixed reactions, including support from some members of the Kansas Education Board who saw his argument as blasphemous. The issue gained widespread attention online and even attracted positive reviews from religious scholars who interpreted the spaghetti monster metaphor as representing different aspects of human anatomy and gender roles.  Henderson\'s stance highlights ongoing debates about teaching creationism in public schools. \n\n\n\n"\n\n\nCONCISE SUMMARY:ë©´ ë¶€ë¶„ì€ ì—¬ì„±ì„ ë‚˜íƒ€ë‚´ë©°, â€˜ëª¨ì–‘â€™ì€ ì„±ë³„ì„ í‘œí˜„í•œë‹¤.â€ë¼ê³  ì„¤ëª…í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì¢…êµì¸ë¥˜í•™ìë“¤ì€ ë‚ ì•„ë‹¤ë‹ˆëŠ” ìŠ¤íŒŒê²Œí‹° ê´´ë¬¼ì„ í†µí•´ ì‹ ì•™ê³¼ ì¸ê°„ ë³¸ì§ˆì— ëŒ€í•´ ë‹¤ê°ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ìƒê°í•´ ë³¼ ìˆ˜ ìˆëŠ” ì¢‹ì€ ë„êµ¬ë¼ëŠ” ì ì„ ê°•ë ¥íˆ ì œì•ˆí•©ë‹ˆë‹¤."\n\n\n\n**Summary:**\n\nA physics professor at Oregon State University, Bobby Henderson, has publicly called for the equal treatment of creationism and evolution in public school biology classes. It was born out of resistance to teaching creationism alongside evolution in public schools. A young physics student named Bobby Henderson proposed that students should be taught about the concept of "critical design," which he argued could be represented by a fictional entity called the "Flying Spaghetti Monster". This idea gained traction when it became an object of ridicule for those who opposed critical thinking and led to its popularization through various media outlets.
